     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      这个我之前写过一篇文章，里面详细介绍了每部分的内容，这个地方再简单的和大家过一下。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     一定不要忽略标准化的价值，当你从底向上把运维标准化做好了，你以后的运维成本会大大的降低，比如说自动化，甚至是服务发现等等。我之前把标准化分成：服务器的、OS的、机房部署的、应用环境的等等。这个里面发挥一下想象力，能标准化就标准化，小到一个进程的属主和路径，达到机房甚至是架构选型。特别是架构选型这块，一定不要被开发牵着走，特别是有些研发说性能很高，我希望你们给到的回复是，我多给你几台服务器。
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      还有一个标准化很重要的是协议，在YY有一个标准化的YY协议，目前我负责的业务这边都采用http协议，在统一协议之上做一些运维能力封装特别简单，比如说监控、数据采集等等。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      服务化，我刚才说mc、mysql都是组件化能力，不是服务化能力，真正服务化的平台一定是运维友好的，一定是对前端应用是无状态感知的，比如说mysql扩容和迁移等等，都可以做到对APP无感知，这才是服务化能力。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      无状态，等我们所有基础设施都标准化了，这个时候，我们就要去无状态化了，去识别架构中的单点问题，挖掘出来优化他。这个里面有方法论可以遵循，早期腾讯有个海量服务运营之道，大家可以网上找找。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      我这次有个项目优化也遵循了这个原则，收到很好的效果。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      应用运维也有了路径，接下来就是怎么落地了，那么我会在不同的阶段，制定不同的方向，比如说我现在的团队来说，我的方向如下：
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <img alt="" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/41c70aa6a61c5c94552f1e7cea99cb70.png" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; max-width:100%; white-space:normal; height:auto!important; word-wrap:break-word!important; visibility:visible!important; width:auto!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; font-size:14px; font-family:宋体; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      </span>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; font-size:14px; font-family:宋体; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      </span>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; font-size:14px; font-family:宋体; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      </span>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; font-size:14px; font-family:宋体; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
      </span>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
        就是做数据化运维、自动化运维和精细化运维。
       </span>
      </span>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      紧扣当前阶段的目标，识别当前团队的矛盾点，设定具体的KPI方向，持续以周为单位进行跟踪。
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       都会有明确的要求，每周滚动。这个群里面很多我的同事。这个地方的建议，一定不要把扩容变更能力、服务器提供能力作为指标放到你的KPI中。做得不透明和不好是我们的耻辱，做得好是应该的。所以很多时候我说运维是要带着耻辱感去工作，每天我做重复的事情，点按钮，敲命令就该想想什么地方要改进了。
      </span>
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     第一部分什么是应用运维我讲完了，什么是应用运维--》整体的指导原则--》应用运维的实现路径---&gt;运维的工作方向---》最后到运维的KPI持续滚动。
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <img alt="" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/646cace24e946cd4c8e34713723b74d9.png" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; max-width:100%; height:auto!important; word-wrap:break-word!important; visibility:visible!important; width:auto!important"/>
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; font-size:14px; font-family:宋体; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      </span>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; font-size:14px; font-family:宋体; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      </span>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      这是运维团队能力要求，里面有三个部分，业务运维即应用运维、运维研发、运维技术研究。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <span class="tn-Powered-by-XIUMI" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; font-size:1em; font-family:inherit; line-height:1.4; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      我希望大家日常的运维工作，在业务运维这块越少越好，而运维研发和技术研究越多越好。
     </span>
     还有一个非常重要的东西，运维工作是什么驱动的，这个代表着不同类型的三种团队。
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; font-size:14px; font-family:宋体; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      </span>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <img alt="" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/9612d99258b0479b879906acd108274a.png" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; max-width:100%; height:auto!important; word-wrap:break-word!important; visibility:visible!important; width:auto!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; font-size:14px; font-family:宋体; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      </span>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      问题驱动，救火队员，你天天在救火，有没有感觉每天半夜要起来苦逼，如果是这样的话，一定要去把问题找出来，这个阶段都有，按照我说的三部走一定可以解决。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     事务和需求驱动，我觉得就是一个保姆角色，做内部服务的提供者，研发找我要服务器，我给服务器，找我部署，我去部署，找我做什么我就干什么。最后一个是价值、优化、用户驱动的运维团队，我们需要走出来，把自己的能力放大一下，运维能做的事情很多呢，三部曲里面那么多东西可以做，还有自动化平台建设，还有数据化平台建设。
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <img alt="" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/8be6700e36458241c952965cb1ec005d.png" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; max-width:100%; height:auto!important; word-wrap:break-word!important; visibility:visible!important; width:auto!important"/>
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <span class="tn-Powered-by-XIUMI" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; font-size:1em; font-family:inherit; line-height:1.4; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      个人能力模型，其实这个是腾讯的职级通道体系里面给的，他分成了10个维度对应用运维提出了要求，其实我觉得写得不是很好，忽略了运维研发能力要求和运维规划能力要求。
     </span>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      特别是T3、T4职级，我觉得一定是从运维研发能力走过来的，只有你做过自动化，你才能对运维的东西进行抽象，其实这个和测试一样，长期做功能测试，你最后都失去了对测试美好愿景的想象，运维也是如此的。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      技术能力希望大家再全栈一点，很多应用运维一个薄弱的环节就是对数据能力的了解。其实我有时候还建议大家去看看Oracle数据库呢，这个能力非常重要。恰恰我觉得应用运维做到最后如果能不了解业务就最好了，做到业务无差异化运维。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      其实运维开始非常苦逼，是吧！但是你把这个事情当成一个挑战来看和对自己的一个不断完美的要求，你会觉得运维是有很多美感的，这个美感我在之前一篇文章里面讲过了。在此就不复述了。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; text-align:center; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <img alt="" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/149160ac34b3cfe2caea4c5ec08e33a6.png" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; max-width:100%; height:auto!important; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; font-family:宋体; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       （图还是要给，强化一下大家对美感的认识）
      </span>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; font-size:14px; font-family:宋体; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
      </span>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      这一部分我讲了团队能力要求，驱动模型，个人能力要求和运维美感，不全是苦逼。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       最后一部分我讲一下一个故障看运维的价值。
      </span>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <img alt="" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/858e166d3a6227f33b11f6e1fbed6189.png" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; max-width:100%; height:auto!important; word-wrap:break-word!important; visibility:visible!important; width:auto!important"/>
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; font-size:14px; font-family:宋体; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      </span>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; font-size:14px; font-family:宋体; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      </span>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; font-family:宋体; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       说一下家丑，去年12月13号，我们一个核心业务，因为交换机故障，导致我们服务终端45分钟，100%服务不可用，耻辱。
      </span>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; font-family:宋体; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
      </span>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; font-family:宋体; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      </span>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; font-family:宋体; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       这个故障暴漏了很多问题，我们有冷备中心用不起来，复盘的时候发现很多架构问题。
      </span>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; font-size:14px; font-family:宋体; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      </span>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; font-size:14px; font-family:宋体; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      </span>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <img alt="" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/1f2be4300afe7743c7616c7a1c171752.png" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; max-width:100%; height:auto!important; word-wrap:break-word!important; visibility:visible!important; width:auto!important"/>
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      问题真的很多很多，这个地方有个经验，问题是运维最好的老师，特别是线上故障，如果一个故障产生的时候，运维一定要挑头把这个故障进行复盘（腾讯运维的经验），最后你能识别出很多需要改进的地方。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <span class="tn-Powered-by-XIUMI" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; font-size:1em; font-family:inherit; line-height:1.4; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      好吧，问题已经发生了，我们要解决它，领导说了，别跟我说那么多没用的，简单指标，5分钟发现故障、三分钟解决。怎么解决啊，几乎是不可能的任务，不过领导说的，咱们硬着头皮也要挑战一下。不过UC有一个很棒的地方，团队合作特别好，一群优秀的人。我们就成立了一个专项组：把产品、测试、运维、研发、还有项目管理都卷进来了。
     </span>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      13号出的故障，14号我们复盘了，15号了，我们就成立项目组了。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <img alt="" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/cccb117c06fd936e15e6b0b0cb949f9d.png" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; max-width:100%; height:auto!important; word-wrap:break-word!important; visibility:visible!important; width:auto!important"/>
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; font-size:14px; font-family:宋体; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      </span>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      简单而极致的要求是我们平时需要不断告诉自己的，最怕的心里状态是这个故障跟我没关系，头都不挑，其次一种怕，就是说技术能力不足，会不会被研发挑战。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
        不要怕呢，我们都是为用户服务的。
       </span>
      </span>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
        <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
       </span>
      </span>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     其实从这个节奏来说，UC的响应速度非常快。
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      我在项目一开始，也确定了一些原则，其中总结起来最核心的就是”技术驱动优化“，而不是流程优化。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <img alt="" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/b5121932b082b9942d89059e1a632c08.png" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; max-width:100%; height:auto!important; word-wrap:break-word!important; visibility:visible!important; width:auto!important"/>
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; font-size:14px; font-family:宋体; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      </span>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      这个里面分成了六个方向：服务降级、双中心、统一调度、过载保护、业务分离、立体化监控。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      为什么需要这些简单的原则？这个有利于项目一致的理解。其实刚刚头条新闻也发生了500错误，从服务影响时间来看，30分钟左右，我猜是后台数据库压力过大导致，在这些原则里面都能找到解决方案，比如说过载保护，服务分离等等。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      这些原则和方向许多都是运维参与的，比如说双中心就涉及到运维参与方案的讨论，给出数据双中心的方案、立体化监控也是80%是运维来做的，统一调度，我们借助了天雷调度（httpdns）。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      然后在这六个方向上我们就制定了具体的改进措施，最终完成了刚才说的5+3目标。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     这个故障其实可以看到运维很多东西可以做的，首先运维一定牵头，第二运维一定要提出自己的要求，第三运维跟进参与整个改进方案的实施，第四，运维要最后给出最终的结果报告，我们做了这么多到底怎么样。
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <img alt="" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/5521141c71f2f391fab6acc7e10fbb02.png" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; max-width:100%; height:auto!important; word-wrap:break-word!important; visibility:visible!important; width:auto!important"/>
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; font-size:14px; font-family:宋体; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      </span>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      自己希望的一个愿景吧，没有操作就是好的运维，最
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       后应用运维没有运维就是好的运维。
      </span>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
      </span>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      其实许多时候不要让大家感受到我们运维，我们运维就是成功了，运维的SAAS化一定是未来的趋势。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <span class="tn-Powered-by-XIUMI" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; font-size:1em; font-family:inherit; line-height:1.4; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      自己也倡导了一些运维理念：
     </span>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <img alt="" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/422511628a05c846b84c12b497804b42.png" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; max-width:100%; height:auto!important; word-wrap:break-word!important; visibility:visible!important; width:auto!important"/>
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; font-size:14px; font-family:宋体; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      </span>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; font-size:14px; font-family:宋体; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      </span>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; font-size:14px; font-family:宋体; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      </span>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
        接下来是
        <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; line-height:24px; word-wrap:break-word!important">
         问答环节
        </span>
        ：
       </span>
      </span>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      1、目前自动化运维这块有什么好的学习建议吗？
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      王：我对自动化有分层化的理解，我建议应用运维第一个把持续集成作为重点，其次是把配置管理作为方向（比如说puppet、saltstack）等等。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      持续集成带来的收益非常大，可以把运维从日常繁琐、低价值的任务中释放出来，并且是跨越了研发、测试和运维三个团队，这个里面解放了几个团队的生产力，收益很大。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     但我建议你们持续集成一定以标准化为前提，否则做起来很累。具体的表述见文章：【平台篇】运维自动化平台深度解码
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      2、问题类似：技术驱动，那些技术？
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     王：这个技术驱动，其实是一些技术的方法论，基于这个方法论，当然你也需要很多的技术储备，无论是存储的、还是应用的，还是协议的，还是程序研发的，甚至是测试的，都需要了解了，全栈。
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      3、请问，很多企业把运维细化到分片分区管理，你说的运维理念又很难实施了。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     王：这个应该是传统企业来的吧，这个变革力就看大家的要求了。我的预见是总有一天用户会逼着你做出改变，这种外力比内力推动力更强。
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      4、具体的学习路线
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     王：如饥似渴的学习和运维相关的一切知识，ITIL、网络的、操作系统、应用组件的.....没有好的学习路线来遵循，把你岗位上做到机制，把周边知识都吸收进来，比如说你从网络上去看应用运维
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      5、学习建议
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      王：我的建议不要浮于表面做运维，当你遇到一个不懂的问题时候，你要深究到底，然后顺着他就可以打开知识体系了，举两个简单的例子，top命令看到的那些CPU占用的指标，user、sys、idle、io....我以前面试就经常问这个，可惜很多人都不知道。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      如果你能说出来原理，就说明你把知识地图打开了。其次我们经常定位问题用的strace，但你真正的去了解strace原理的时候，里面有很多操作系统的知识涉及到，当年因为strace，我还把操作系统的书重新看了一遍。不放过任何一个细节，总结和思考自己目前正在做的。我觉得其他的东西都好解决了。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      6、请教：运维人如何做绩效考核？东西很难量化，主观意识太强？
     </p>
     <div>
      <br/>
     </div>
     <br/>

    </div>

     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      由于自己一直是做应用运维的，所以今天主要是和大家讲应用运维相关的，我个人总结了一些体系和方法论，希望能对你们有帮助。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">

     </p>

      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <span class="tn-Powered-by-XIUMI" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; font-size:1em; font-family:inherit; line-height:1.4; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      第一部分：我讲应用运维是什么；
     </span>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      第二部分：我讲应用运维需要什么样的团队；
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      第三部分：给个案例讲讲运维能做什么？
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; white-space:pre-wrap; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       <strong style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
        <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; line-height:22px; word-wrap:break-word!important">
         第一部分：应用运维是什么
        </span>
       </strong>
      </span>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       <strong style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
        <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; line-height:22px; word-wrap:break-word!important">
         <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
        </span>
       </strong>
      </span>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; color:rgb(51,51,51); max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,'Hiragino Sans GB','Microsoft YaHei',微软雅黑,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:18px; orphans:2; widows:2; line-height:1.5em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      其实很多时候非运维的人员不知道运维是什么，他们都理解你们是网管、提供服务器的，处理故障的，其实这些都不是。
     </p>
